                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-gu4dR1Vvyf4/VTpHcatY2tI/AAAAAAAAB5A/TNrcDo7OiO4/s1600/Magnetic%2Bfield-appr24-4-15.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                        <br/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                         Questions involving
 magnetic fields
                        </span>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style="color: #943634; mso-themecolor: accent2; mso-themeshade: 191;">
                         are generally simple and interesting. But
 questions which appear simple at the first glance may tempt you to commit
 mistakes.
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style="color: #943634; mso-themecolor: accent2; mso-themeshade: 191;">
                         Here are a few
 multiple choice practice questions (single correct answer type) in this section:
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                         (1) An electron is projected at right angles to a uniform
 magnetic field. The quantity that remains constant is
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (a) velocity of electron
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (b) momentum of electron
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (c) kinetic energy of electron
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (d) all the above
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         The velocity and momentum of the electron get
 changed since the direction of motion of the electron within the magnetic field
 changes continuously. However, the kinetic energy of the electron remains
 constant since the magnitudes of the velocity and momentum remain constant.
 Therefore, the correct option is (c).
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (2)
                        </span>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                         An electron is projected
 at right angles to a magnetic field that changes in magnitude with time. The
 quantity that remains constant is
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (a) kinetic energy of electron
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (b) momentum of electron
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (c) velocity of electron
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (d) none of the above
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style="color: #943634; mso-themecolor: accent2; mso-themeshade: 191;">
                         Since
 the magnetic field is changing, an emf is induced. The speed of the electron is
 changed and therefore the velocity, momentum and the kinetic energy are
 changed.
                        </span>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         The correct option is (d).
                        </span>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style="color: #943634; mso-themecolor: accent2; mso-themeshade: 191;">
                         <span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: #00b050; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                         [Note
 that the particle accelerator
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          betatron
                         </i>
                         works on the principle of the production of an accelerating emf due to a
 changing magnetic field]
                        </span>
                        <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-gu4dR1Vvyf4/VTpHcatY2tI/AAAAAAAAB5A/TNrcDo7OiO4/s1600/Magnetic%2Bfield-appr24-4-15.jpg" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;">
                         <img border="0" height="287" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-gu4dR1Vvyf4/VTpHcatY2tI/AAAAAAAAB5A/TNrcDo7OiO4/s1600/Magnetic%2Bfield-appr24-4-15.jpg" width="320"/>
                        </a>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: #00b050; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>

                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (3) Two very long straight conductors are arranged perpendicular to the
 XY plane. Their mid points are at A and B and are at the same distance ‘
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          a
                         </i>
                         ’ from the origin (Fig.). Each
 conductor carries a current ‘
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          I
                         </i>
                         ’ in
 the negative z-direction. What is the direction of the resultant magnetic field
 at the origin?
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (a) along OP
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (b) along OQ
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (c) along OR
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (d) along OS
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                         The
 magnetic field produced at the origin O by the current in the conductor located
 at A is directed along OY.
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: #00b050; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                         [Note that
 the current is directed normally into the plane of the figure. You may use
 Maxwell’s cork screw rule or the right hand palm rule to obtain the direction
 of the magnetic field].
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                         The
 magnetic field produced at the origin O by the current in the conductor located
 at B is directed along OX’. Since the magnetic fields produced at O by the two
 conductors are of the same magnitude, the resultant magnetic field at O is
 equally inclined to OY and OX’ and is directed along OP.
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         4) In question No. (3) the magnitude of the resultant magnetic flux
 density at the origin O is
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (a)
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          μ
                          <sub>
                           0
                          </sub>
                          I
                         </i>
                         /2π
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          a
                         </i>
                         <b>
                         </b>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (b) (√2)
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          μ
                          <sub>
                           0
                          </sub>
                          I
                         </i>
                         /2π
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          a
                         </i>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (c)
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          μ
                          <sub>
                           0
                          </sub>
                          I
                         </i>
                         /π
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          a
                         </i>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (d) 2
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          μ
                          <sub>
                           0
                          </sub>
                          I
                         </i>
                         /π
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          a
                         </i>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                         The
 magnetic flux density at distance
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          a
                         </i>
                         from a long conductor carrying current
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          I
                         </i>
                         is
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          <span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">
                           μ
                           <sub>
                            0
                           </sub>
                           I
                          </span>
                         </i>
                         <span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">
                          /2π
                          <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                           a
                          </i>
                          . Therefore, the resultant magnetic
 flux density at the origin O due to the two flux densities directed along OY
 and OX’ which are at right angles is
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: maroon; font-size: 12pt;">
                           √[(
                          </span>
                          <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                           <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue; font-size: 12pt;">
                           </span>
                           <span lang="EN-US" style="color: maroon; font-size: 12pt;">
                            μ
                            <sub>
                             0
                            </sub>
                            I
                           </span>
                          </i>
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: maroon; font-size: 12pt;">
                           /2π
                           <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                            a
                           </i>
                           )
                           <sup>
                            2
                           </sup>
                           + (
                          </span>
                          <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                           <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue; font-size: 12pt;">
                           </span>
                           <span lang="EN-US" style="color: maroon; font-size: 12pt;">
                            μ
                            <sub>
                             0
                            </sub>
                            I
                           </span>
                          </i>
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: maroon; font-size: 12pt;">
                           /2π
                           <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                            a
                           </i>
                           )
                           <sup>
                            2
                           </sup>
                           ]
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         = (√2)
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          μ
                          <sub>
                           0
                          </sub>
                          I
                         </i>
                         /2π
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          a
                         </i>
                         , as given in option (b).
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (5) A bar magnet placed in a non-uniform magnetic field will experience
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (a) a torque, but no net force
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (b) a net force, but no torque
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (c) neither a net force nor a torque
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (d) a net force as well as a torque
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         If a bar magnet is located in a uniform magnetic
 field, the poles of the magnet will experience forces of equal magnitude, but
 of
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          opposite
                         </i>
                         direction. The net force
 acting on the magnet will therefore be zero. But the two equal and opposite
 forces will produce a torque which will try to rotate the bar magnet. If the
 magnetic field is non-uniform, the forces acting on the poles of the magnet
 will be of unequal magnitude so that in addition to a torque, there will be a
 net force on the magnet [Option (d)].
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-gu4dR1Vvyf4/VTpHcatY2tI/AAAAAAAAB5A/TNrcDo7OiO4/s1600/Magnetic%2Bfield-appr24-4-15.jpg" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;">
                      </a>

   <w:LsdException Locked="false" Priority="61" SemiHidden="false"
    UnhideWhenUsed="false" Name="Light List Accent 2"/>
   <w:LsdException Locked="false" Priority="62" SemiHidden="false"
    UnhideWhenUsed="false" Name="Light Grid Accent 2"/>
   <w:LsdException Locked="false" Priority="63" SemiHidden="false"
    UnhideWhenUsed="false" Name="Medium Shading 1 Accent 2"/>
   <w:LsdException Locked="false" Priority="64" SemiHidden="false"
    UnhideWhenUsed="false" Name="Medium Shading 2 Accent 2"/>
   <w:LsdException Locked="false" Priority="65" SemiHidden="false"
    UnhideWhenUsed="false" Name="Medium List 1 Accent 2"/>

                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span lang="EN-US" style='color: red; font-family: "Arial","sans-serif";'>
                        “One of the deep
 secrets of life is that all that is really worth the doing is what we do for
 others.”
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span lang="EN-US" style='color: red; font-family: "Arial","sans-serif";'>
                        – Lewis Carroll
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                         As you
 know, with effect from the academic year 2014 – 2015, AP Physics B course is
 discontinued and is replaced by two new courses, namely AP Physics 1 and AP
 Physics 2. Both courses are algebra based. It is hoped that the new courses
 will help the students to explore deeper into key concepts in physics both in
 theory and practice.
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                         Today we
 shall discuss a few multiple choice practice questions relevant to AP Physics 1
 and AP Physics 2 courses. Questions (1), (2) and (3) are for AP Physics 1 where
 as questions (4) , (5) and (6) are for AP Physics 2.
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                         Questions
 (1) and (2) are single correct answer type multiple choice questions where as question
 (3) is multi-correct answer type multiple choice question.
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                         Similarly
 questions (4) and (5) are single correct answer type multiple choice questions
 where as question (6) is multi-correct answer type multiple choice question.
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                          (1)
                         </span>
                        </b>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                         The magnitude of the gravitational force on a
 solid sphere A of radius
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          R
                         </i>
                         and
 density
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          d
                         </i>
                         at a point P in the earth’s
 atmosphere is
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          F
                         </i>
                         . If this sphere is
 replaced by another solid sphere B of radius 2
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          R
                         </i>
                         and density 2
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          d
                         </i>
                         , the
 magnitude of the gravitational force acting on it will be
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (a) 2
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          F
                         </i>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (b) 4
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          F
                         </i>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (c) 8
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          F
                         </i>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (d) 16
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          F
                         </i>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <b>
                         <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                          (2)
                         </span>
                        </b>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         The sphere A in question number (1) starts to fall freely under earth’s
 gravity with an acceleration of magnitude
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          g
                         </i>
                         <sub>
                          1
                         </sub>
                         .
 What will be the magnitude of the acceleration of free fall of sphere B under
 earth’s gravity?
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (a)
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          g
                         </i>
                         <sub>
                          1
                         </sub>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (b) 2
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          g
                         </i>
                         <sub>
                          1
                         </sub>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         (c) 4
                         <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                          g
                         </i>
                         <sub>
                          1
                         </sub>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                       <span lang="EN-US" style="clear: right; color: blue; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;">
                       </span>
                       <span style="font-size: small;">
                        <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                         <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                          (d) 16
                          <i>
                           g
                          </i>
                          <sub>
                           1
                          </sub>

                       <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                        <br/>
                        <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                         <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                          <b>
                           <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                            (3)
                           </span>
                          </b>
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                           A loud speaker is excited with an alternating current of frequency 1000
 Hz. The sound produced by the loud speaker propagates in air along the x-axis
 through points P and Q (Fig.), which lie 5 m apart. Which of the following
 statements are true in this context?
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </div>
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         <span style="font-size: small;">
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                        <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                         <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                           (a) Air molecules at P and Q vibrate parallel to the x-axis
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </div>
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         <span style="font-size: small;">
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                        <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                         <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                           (b) The speed of sound at Q is less than the speed at P since Q is at a
 greater distance from the loud speaker.
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </div>
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         <span style="font-size: small;">
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                        <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                         <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                           (c) Air molecules at P are carried along the x-axis to the point Q and
 then farther away from Q.
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </div>
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         <span style="font-size: small;">
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                        <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                         <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                           (d) Air molecules at P and Q always maintain their mean positions at P
 and Q.
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </div>
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         <span style="font-size: small;">
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                        <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                         <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                          <br/>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </div>
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         <span style="font-size: small;">
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                        <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                         <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                          <b>
                           <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                            (4)
                           </span>
                          </b>
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                           An electron is projected with uniform velocity
                           <b>
                            v
                           </b>
                           along the axis
 of a plane circular coil carrying a steady current. Which one among the
 following statements is correct?
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </div>
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia,"Times New Roman",serif;'>
                        <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                         <span style="font-size: small;">
                         </span>
                         <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                           (a) The electron will continue to move along the axis with uniform
 acceleration
                          </span>
                         </div>
                         <span style="font-size: small;">
                         </span>
                         <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                           (b) The electron will move along a helical path around the axis of the
 circular coil.
                          </span>
                         </div>
                         <span style="font-size: small;">
                         </span>
                         <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                           (c) The electron will continue to move along the axis with uniform
 acceleration or deceleration, depending on the direction of the current in the
 coil
                          </span>
                         </div>
                         <span style="font-size: small;">
                         </span>
                         <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                           (d) The electron will continue to move along the axis with uniform
 velocity
                           <b>
                            v
                           </b>
                          </span>
                         </div>
                         <span style="font-size: small;">
                         </span>
                         <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                          <br/>
                         </div>
                         <span style="font-size: small;">
                         </span>
                         <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                          <b>
                           <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                            (5)
                           </span>
                          </b>
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                           A beam of sun light is allowed to fall normally on one face of a glass
 slab of uniform thickness. Light of which component colour will emerge
                           <i>
                            last
                           </i>
                           through the opposite face of the
 slab?
                          </span>
                         </div>
                         <span style="font-size: small;">
                         </span>
                         <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                           (a) Green
                          </span>
                         </div>
                         <span style="font-size: small;">
                         </span>
                         <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                           (b) Red
                          </span>
                         </div>
                         <span style="font-size: small;">
                         </span>
                         <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                           (c) Violet
                          </span>
                         </div>
                         <span style="font-size: small;">
                         </span>
                         <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                           (d) All colours will emerge simultaneously
                          </span>
                          <br/>
