                          <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                           <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                            <a href="https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/-_zrDRme4tNw/U-83SofZofI/AAAAAAAAB4M/IIlOT3YbXS4/h37/Waves2-appr16-8-14.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;">
                             <img alt="" border="0" class="Yl-O-x" height="33" src="https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/-_zrDRme4tNw/U-83SofZofI/AAAAAAAAB4M/IIlOT3YbXS4/h37/Waves2-appr16-8-14.jpg" style="left: 0px; top: 0px; transform: rotate(0deg);" width="320"/>
                            </a>
                            <b>
                             <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                              (6)
                             </span>
                            </b>
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             S is a police vehicle which sounds a siren and L is a listener in a car
 on a straight road. In which of the following cases will the listener L note an
 apparent increase in the frequency of the sound emitted by the siren?
                            </span>
                           </span>
                          </div>
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                          </span>
                          <br/>
                          <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                           <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             (a) S and L moving in the direction S
                             <span style="font-size: xx-small;">
                              L
                             </span>
                             with speeds 2
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              u
                             </i>
                             and
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              u
                             </i>
                             respectively.
                            </span>
                           </span>
                          </div>
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                          </span>
                          <br/>
                          <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                           <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             (b) S and L moving in the direction L
                             <span style="font-size: xx-small;">
                              S
                             </span>
                             with speeds
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              u
                             </i>
                             and 2
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              u
                             </i>
                             respectively.
                            </span>
                           </span>
                          </div>
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                          </span>
                          <br/>
                          <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                           <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             (c) S and L moving in the direction S
                             <span style="font-size: xx-small;">
                              L
                             </span>
                             with speeds
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              u
                             </i>
                             and 2
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              u
                             </i>
                             respectively
                            </span>
                           </span>
                          </div>
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                          </span>
                          <br/>
                          <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                           <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             (d) S and L stationary and wind blowing in the direction S
                             <span style="font-size: xx-small;">
                              L
                             </span>
                             with speed
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              u
                             </i>
                             .
                            </span>
                           </span>
                          </div>
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                          </span>
                          <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                           <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                            <br/>
                           </span>
                          </div>
                          <span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue;">
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             Now, let us answer the above questions:
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <b>
                             <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                              (1)
                             </span>
                            </b>
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             The gravitational force is directly proportional to
 the mass of the sphere. The mass of sphere A is (4/3) π
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              R
                             </i>
                             <span style="font-size: small;">
                              <sup>
                               3
                              </sup>
                             </span>
                             d where as the mass of sphere B is (4/3) π(2
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              R
                             </i>
                             )
                             <sup>
                              3
                             </sup>
                             (2
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              d
                             </i>
                             ) = 16(4/3) π
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              R
                             </i>
                             <sup>
                              3
                             </sup>
                             d.
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             Since the mass of sphere B is 16 times the mass of A
 the gravitational force on B is 16 times that on A. The answer is 16
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              F
                             </i>
                             [Option (d)].
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <br/>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <b>
                             <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                              (2)
                             </span>
                            </b>
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             Acceleration = Force/Mass.
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             Even though the gravitational force on sphere B is
 16 times that on sphere A, the acceleration of sphere B is the same as that of
 sphere A since the mass of sphere B is 16 times that of sphere A. The answer is
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              g
                             </i>
                             <sub>
                              1
                             </sub>
                             [Option (a)].
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <br/>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <b>
                             <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                              (3)
                             </span>
                            </b>
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             Sound is a longitudinal wave. In longitudinal waves
 particles of the medium vibrate parallel to the direction of propagation of the
 wave. Option
                             <b>
                              (a) is correct
                             </b>
                             . When a wave propagates through a medium,
 particles of the medium just vibrate about their position and are
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              not carried
                             </i>
                             along with the wave
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              .
                             </i>
                             Therefore, option
                             <b>
                              (d) is correct
                             </b>
                             and (c) is incorrect. The speed of a wave depends only on the properties of the
 medium through which the wave propagates. Therefore, option (b) is incorrect.
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <br/>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <b>
                             <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                              (4)
                             </span>
                            </b>
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             The magnetic field due to a current carrying
 circular coil at any point on its axis is directed along the axis. Therefore,
 the electron projected along the axis of the coil moves either parallel or
 anti-parallel to the direction of the magnetic field produced by the coil. Consequently
 the magnetic force on the electron is zero.
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: #00b050; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             [The expression for the magnitude of the magnetic
 force
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              F
                             </i>
                             on a moving charge is
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              F = qvB
                             </i>
                             sin
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              θ
                             </i>
                             where
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              q
                             </i>
                             is the charge,
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              v
                             </i>
                             is the speed of the charge,
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              B
                             </i>
                             is the magnitude of the magnetic flux
 density and
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              θ
                             </i>
                             is the angle between
 the direction of motion of the charge and the direction of the magnetic field.
 In the present case
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              θ
                             </i>
                             is either zero
 or 180º so that sin
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              θ
                             </i>
                             is zero].
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                             The
 electron will therefore be unaffected and will continue to move with uniform
 velocity
                             <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                              v
                             </b>
                             [Option (d)].
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <br/>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                             <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                              (5)
                             </span>
                            </b>
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                             Violet light has
 the least speed in a material medium. Therefore, light of violet colour will
 emerge last from the opposite face of the slab [Option (c)].
                            </span>
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: #00b050; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: #00b050; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             [Note that the refractive index of a material medium
 for violet light is maximum (since violet light is bent most). Since the
 refractive index of a medium is the ratio of the speed of light in free space
 to the speed in the medium, it follows that the speed is smaller if the
 refractive index is greater].
                            </span>
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                             <span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">
                             </span>
                             <span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">
                             </span>
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <br/>
                            <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                             <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                              (6)
                             </span>
                            </b>
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                             This
 question involves Doppler effect, which is the
                            </span>
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: red; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                            </span>
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             phenomenon by which the frequency of a
 wave as measured by an observer is changed because of the motion of the source,
 observer and the medium.
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             Let the source S of sound (fig.) move with velocity
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              v
                             </i>
                             <sub>
                              S
                             </sub>
                             , the listener move with
 velocity
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              v
                             </i>
                             <sub>
                              L
                             </sub>
                             and the wind
 blow with velocity
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              w
                             </i>
                             , all in the
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              same
                             </i>
                             direction as shown in the figure.
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <br/>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             <span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">
                             </span>
                            </span>
                            <span style="color: black;">
                             <b>
                              <span lang="EN-US" style='mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                               Wind→ w
                               <span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">
                               </span>
                               S●→
                               <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                                v
                               </i>
                               <span style="font-size: xx-small;">
                                <sub>
                                 S
                                </sub>
                               </span>
                               <span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">
                               </span>
                               L●→
                               <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                                v
                               </i>
                               <span style="font-size: xx-small;">
                                <sub>
                                 L
                                </sub>
                               </span>
                              </span>
                             </b>
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <br/>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             The apparent frequency (
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              n’
                             </i>
                             ) of sound is then given by
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             <span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">
                             </span>
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              n’ = n
                             </i>
                             (
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              v + w
                             </i>
                            </span>
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                             –
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              <span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">
                               v
                              </span>
                             </i>
                             <span style="font-size: xx-small;">
                              <sub>
                               L
                              </sub>
                             </span>
                             <span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">
                              )/ (
                              <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                               v +
 w
                              </i>
                             </span>
                             –
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              <span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">
                               v
                              </span>
                             </i>
                             <span style="font-size: xx-small;">
                              <sub>
                               S
                              </sub>
                             </span>
                             <span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">
                              ) ………………………(i)
                             </span>
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             where
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              n
                             </i>
                             is
 the real frequency of the sound and
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              v
                             </i>
                             is the velocity of sound. It may be noted that the above relation has been
 derived on the assumption that the source is moving towards the listener, the
 listener is moving
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              away from
                             </i>
                             the
 source and the wind is blowing
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              from the
 source to the listener
                             </i>
                             .
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                             </i>
                             <span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">
                             </span>
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             Considering case (a), we have
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              n’ = n
                             </i>
                             (
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              v +
                             </i>
                             0
                            </span>
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                             –
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              <span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">
                               u
                              </span>
                             </i>
                             <span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">
                              )/ (
                              <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                               v +
                              </i>
                              0
                              <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              </i>
                             </span>
                             –
                             <span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">
                              2
                              <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                               u
                              </i>
                              )
 so that
                              <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                               n’ &gt; n
                              </i>
                             </span>
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             Considering case (b), we have
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              n’ = n
                             </i>
                             (
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              v +
                             </i>
                             0
                            </span>
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                             + 2
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              <span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">
                               u
                              </span>
                             </i>
                             <span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">
                              )/ (
                              <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                               v +
                              </i>
                              0
                              <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              </i>
                             </span>
                             +
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              <span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">
                               u
                              </span>
                             </i>
                             <span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">
                              ) so that
                              <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                               n’
 &gt; n
                              </i>
                             </span>
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: #00b050; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             [Note that the signs of
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              v
                             </i>
                             <sub>
                              L
                             </sub>
                             and
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              v
                             </i>
                             <sub>
                              S
                             </sub>
                             are negative in this case]
                            </span>
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             Considering case (c), we have
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              n’ = n
                             </i>
                             (
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              v +
                             </i>
                             0
                            </span>
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                             – 2
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              <span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">
                               u
                              </span>
                             </i>
                             <span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">
                              )/ (
                              <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                               v +
                              </i>
                              0
                              <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              </i>
                             </span>
                             –
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              <span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">
                               u
                              </span>
                             </i>
                             <span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">
                              ) so that
                              <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                               n’
 &lt; n
                              </i>
                             </span>
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             Considering case (d), we have
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              n’ = n
                             </i>
                             (
                             <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                              v + w
                             </i>
                            </span>
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                             – 0
                             <span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">
                              )/ (
                              <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                               v +
 w
                              </i>
                             </span>
                             – 0
                             <span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">
                              ) so that
                              <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                               n’ = n
                              </i>
                             </span>
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: maroon; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman";'>
                             Thus
 cases (a) and (b) are the correct options.
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 36.0pt; text-align: justify;">
                            <span lang="EN-US" style='color: #00b050; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;'>
                             [Even if you don’t remember the above expression
 (i), you will be able to answer many questions if you note that the apparent
 frequency increases if the source moves towards the listener (relatively) or
 the listener moves towards the source (relatively). If they move away from each
 other, the apparent frequency decreases].
                            </span>
                           </div>
                           <div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.75pt 331.5pt 335.25pt 371.25pt 373.5pt; text-align: justify;">

   <w:LsdException Locked="false" Priority="9" QFormat="true" Name="heading 6"/>

   <w:LsdException Locked="false" Priority="39" Name="toc 4"/>
